0a1(rgyud): ni blo can gyis// dus gsum du yang skyabs su 'gro/ dus gsum du ni sdig pa gshegs// dus gsum byang chub seMs kyang skyed/ brgyud mthong chog shes pa yi/ dus bsu du yang smon / 
0a2(rgyud): btab/ cho gar spyod pa de dang der/ ji ltar spyod pa tsi nus bya// rtag tu gtong la brtson pa dang // 'jungs bral snying rjer ldan pa dang / rtag tu bzod cing byams par ldan/ rtag tu brtson 'gyu/ 
0a3(rgyud): ldan par bya/ rjes su dran pa drug rnams kyang / bsam pa de bas rtag tu sgom/ rnam pa sna tshogs chos mnyan nas/ mos par rnam par spyad par bya/ gsang sngags cho ga zhi ba blag/ 
0a4(rgyud): cing sngags dang phyag rgya rnaMs kyang mchod/ dag las ni 'byung ba bzhi/ blo dang ldan pas dkyil 'khor bri// yang dag lta ba nges 'gyur cing // byang chub so sa ni
0a5(rgyud): brtan byas pa/ dge slong la sogs 'khyer ba ni rnams/ mkhas pas rtag ratu bzud par bya// dam tshig phyag bcings nas su/ rang gi gsang sngags rgyud rnams/ 
0a6(rgyud): stan// mkhas pa'i gseng sngags lung gi rnas/ thos cad yang dag rgyas par bya/ sgrub pa pos ni ches rgya dram/ bcu bzhi dang ni bcwo lnga dang / cho 'phrul gyi ni zla byed dam// khyad
0a7(rgyud): pAr du ni mchod pa bya// bzlas brjod sbyin sreg mchod pa dang // de bzhin sdom pa bzung ba dang / khyad par du yang bsod nams la/ gus shing mngon par brdzun par bya// mkhas pas snga/ 
0a8(rgyud): ni 'di nyid kyis/ brgya'am yang na steng dag tu/ mngon par sngags par bya ba yi/ las kyi rdo rje rtag tu bcing/ oM du 'adz+rad/ gnam lcags phog pa'i shing dag gom/ rnam pa 'am/ 
0b1(rgyud): dung khrod 'bram dum 'am/ bcan dan dag gam/ gzhan yang rung / rdo rje rtse mo gsum pa bya// legs pa gyur ces bya ba/ de ni blo ldan lag g.yon gyis/ bzlas rjod sbyin
0b2(rgyud): sreg la seMms pa'i/ skyes su de ni bzung par bya/ rdo rje de ni bcad pa yis/ 'bregs dang log 'dren rdzas cad dang / gang dag gnod pa rnyed pa nas/ shin tu sgrug nas byer bar 'a
0b3(rgyud): de yang gsang sngags de nyid kyis/ mkhas po rtag tu mchod par bya/ btsun dan dmar pos skus nas ni/ gzhag sde mngon par sngags kyis zlas/ las kyi rdo rje zhes bya ba/

8b7(rgyud): dam pa ni/ gang gi rgyun du bshad pa yin// dad dbang la sogs sems gang yi ni// rab lngar na yang dag byung // rnam pa thar pa bzhi pa ni// sgo rnams ni yang dag bshad// yang dog

9a1(rgyud): byang chub yan lag bdun pa ni// 'phreng ba me tog chun rgyan pa// 'phags lam yan lag rgyad pa ni// bka' ba brgyad ces bya bar bshad// sgrib pa gnyis las rnam
9a2(rgyud): zhing // ting 'dzin ye shes kyis rtags pa// lam gi ye shes khyad par rnams// lnga yab ces ni yang dag bshad// nyon mongs ces ni nges gcod cing // nyon mongs 'phrog pas dra ba ste/ 
9a3(rgyud): yang dag gcod cing spong ba nyid// sel ba'i spong ba lnga gnas pa// tshogs gnyis kyi ni sbyor ba nyid// nyon mongs pa'i phyed 'phrog pa// phra ba phyed ces bya bar bshad// rang bzhin 'od
9a4(rgyud): gsalnga gang yin te// byang chub sems ni bla mA da yan// sems ni dron kun skyong byed pa// bzla ba'i dkyil 'khor yan par bshad// shes rab ye shes rang bzhin dgra/ rje rje
9a5(rgyud): lte bu'i ting 'dzin skyes// thar pa'i snang ba gzi rje de rme/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'kho yin par bshad// mtshon rtsi lngar ni yang dag bshad// lta bA lnga yis me tog yin// ye shes/ 
9a6(rgyud): lnga yos nges sbyar nyid// sangs rgyas lnga zhes yang dge bshad// na mkha' bzhin du bdag med pa'i// rnam shes ye shes dam pa yin// ye shes de'i rkyen bshad pa/ chags pa'i
9a7(rgyud): nis bya bar bshad// chags bral las ni byang chub 'byung // chags pa'i sems las gzhan yin no// de bas chags dang chags bral ba// byang chub sems zhes yang dag bshad/ 
9a8(rgyud): 'jig rten chags dang dral bas dul/ phyog rgya'i dngos bya chags las byung // de nin thabs kyi snyoms pa dag / dngos grub thams cad sder po yin/ ji ltar 'jig rten 'dul 'gyur ro/ 
9b1(rgyud): de ltar rnal 'byor pa yis bshad// ci ltar dul bya dag gyur pa// zhen pa kun tu chod par 'gyur// mtshan nyid gang zhig yang dag bshad// mtshan nyid des ni mtshon par 'gyur// sku gsung // 
9b2(rgyud): thugs kyi phyag rgyu yis// rgyas btab ye shes yin par bshad// phyag rgya sgoms pas rnal 'byor pa// rtag tu phyag rgyu'i bdag can gyur// rgyus btab dngos po shes nas ni// skyes nas
9b3(rgyud): phyag rgyas btab par 'gyur// mtshan dang mtshan nyid 'brel ba yo ni// shes nas rnal 'byor yang dag spyod// ci ltar mtshan nyid yang dag grub// de bzhin dag pa myur du 'gyub// g.yas
9b4(rgyud): pA'i cha ni mtshan ma ni// shes rab can na rab tu rAn// gA yon gyi mtshan ma ci ltar mthong / de'i thugs rje mtshon pa yA// phyag ni gnyis klu mnyam sbyor bas// 
9b5(rgyud): ting 'dzin gnyisu bshad pa ya ni// zhabs gnyis kyis nI mtshan ma yis// tshogs gnyis dag ni rten pa yin// sor mo lnga'i maHmau sbyor bas// dkyil 'khor lnga yis
9b6(rgyud): rgyan pa yin// sangs rgya sna lnga yi sti mngon byang chub// rim pa bzhin du sten bya ste// grang zhig gung mo ston pa ni// na mkha' las ni byung ba mtshon// grang zhig 'dzub mo bston pa ni// des ni
9b7(rgyud): dbang chen dkyil 'khor yin// sprin lag tu ni yang dgra bshad// myu'i dkyil 'khor zhes bshad do// gang zhig mthe bong ston pa ni// de'i yis me ni mtshan po yin// gang zhig mthe'u chung
9b8(rgyud): ston pa ni// rlung gi dkyil 'khor nyid du 'gyur// gang zhig lte ba ston pa ni// rdo rje dbyings ga dbang phyug bshad// gang zhig snying kha ston pa ni// rdo rje sems dpa' rje su dag/ gang zhig sngon
10a1(rgyud): 'arnams ston pa ni/ rdo rje ni chen ma zhes bya/ gang zhig lkog ma ston pa ni// rdo rje chos mar shes par bya// glang nig skye bo ston pa ni/ rdo rje lasna mar shes par bya/ 
10a2(rgyud): byu nu ba lngar mngon byang chub bam// yung na ye shes lha rnams sam// sangs rgyas lnga dang yang dag ldan// dkyil 'khor byang chub yin par ston// stan kyi spya na ji ltar bshad// mdun
10a3(rgyud): tu de ni rab tu stan// rmya ba gi sgran ci ltar bshad// hU~M myur de ni yang dag ston// gang du thog ma'i ster gyur paM/ der ni rgyu'i sbyang ru stan// gang zhig mther ma'i sgrar gyur pa/ 'dir ni 'bros
10a4(rgyud): bur yang dag stan// sangs rgyas bcom ldan gnyis mi/ mnga'// rgyu dang 'bras bur ldan gyur mini// gang zhig thog/ ma mtha' ma med// de phyir rtag pa zhes bshad do// 
10a5(rgyud): rAng sems rtogs pas sangs rgyas te// rtogs par bya ba 'ang sos nyid yin// sangs rgyas zhing zhes bshad pa dag/ byang chub semasu bshad par bya// rang bzhin dag pa'i
10a6(rgyud): sos rgyun ni// kun rig+h+ra par yang dag bshad// seMs can rang ba zhin dag pa yin// byang chub sems su shes par bya// dang bar gyur pa snying kar 'debs// bADUn+d+ha pa nyid du'ang rang nyid 'gyur/ 
10a7(rgyud): sgra 'dzin pa ni ril pa'i dbus// 'od dpag med du gtam gnag yin// bcum pa nar ni rjes bshad pa// de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje gsung // dbang po gnyis ni mnyam sbyor ba// rnam par
10a8(rgyud): mdzad ces bshad do// bu mo lo grangs bcu gnyis par// skyes mchog thub pa'i gang gsungs pa// pha rol phyin pa bcu gnyis su// gsung gis gzhan du mi rtagro g+ho/ bu mo lho grangs bcu drug pa
10b1(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pas gang gsungs pa// rdo rje sems bsdogs seMs dpa' yi// sgom pa'i don gyi sgra yin no// lha mo lo grangs nyi shu bar// 'khor sgyur bso 'di skad gsungs// mchod pa nyi shu'i
10b2(rgyud): bdag nyid can// nyi shu dang po rims bzhin no// rang gi chung ma rang rig las// 'byung bas rang rig yin par bshad// gzhan gi chung mar gang stan po// gzhan bstug gzhan gi rig pa yin// TI drang
10b3(rgyud): rdo rje zhes bshad pa// rdo rje ye shes bla med yin// bshang dang phrad ma zhes gshad pa// chos kyi ye shes bla med yin// yongs su gasngal bar rnams shes pa// dkyil 'khor thugs kyi dam/ 
10b4(rgyud): pa yin// sku gsung thugs kyi spyod pa yis// 'ab dA pa yis ni mchod byed pa// rang gi rdo rje pad mer ldan// dbang po gnyis las byung ba yi// rang gi khu ba thig le ya sa// 
10b5(rgyud): rdo rje sras dpa' mchod par bya// tshogs gnyis kyi ni sbyor ba yis// sangs rgyas thos cad gcig skyes pa// gnyis med gnyis nyid la rten pa// thugs rje shugs dang yang dag ldan// dbang
10b6(rgyud): po gnyis kyi nyams sbyor bas// rang gi khu ba mkhas pa yis// rnal 'byor chen po phyug nas ni// dkyil 'khor yang dag byin gyis rlabs// dgod dam rab tu smra ba 'am/ sangs rgyas rol mye'i ger byed pa
10b7(rgyud): lha mo bzhi'i mnyam sbyor bar// rgyu dang mi rgyu nas rol// gsar zhing legs par sgril ba dang // tshad dang ldan zhing mdzes pa yis// shes rab can gyi thig btab pa// sku gsung thugs kyi ni skos pas so// 
10b8(rgyud): zur bzhi pa la sgo bzhi pa// brta babs bzhis ni mdzes byas la// thig bzhi dang ni yang dag ldan// dar dang me tog 'phreng bas rgyan// bgra'i 'tshams ni thams cad dang // sgo khyud kyi ni mtshams rnams/ 
11a1(rgyud): rdo rje rin chen smras pan+d+ha nA~M// b+hi'i dkyil 'khor thig lde gdab po// rdo rje thig gI yongs sbyor cing // bka' ba brgyad kyis nye bar mdzes// bka' ba brgyad kyi nang gnas par/ 
11a2(rgyud): dkyil 'khor rgyad par bstan pa dang // grwa'i dkyil 'khor dor bar ni// rdo rje lha ma tshogs kyis mchod// 'khor lo lnga dang yang dgra ldan// dkyil 'khor lnga yis rnam par rgyan// dra ba dra phyed kyis
11a3(rgyud): spras shing // brda yab kyis ni nyer spras pa// 'khru ni bcu gnyis bya ba 'am// 'khru bcu drug tu rab tu rtag/ yang na khru na nyi shu tsama?// nyi shu lnga dang ldan pa yang sa// 'khru ni ny+dzi shu lnga pa yi// 
11a4(rgyud): dkyil 'khor yang dag byin gyis rlab// sgo rnams kyi ni dbus mi'i cha// chu dgu ru ni rnam dbye' baM// dkyil 'khor sgo ru bas se nas ni// sgo khyud der ni bya ba yan// sgo khyud dkyil
11a5(rgyud): 'khor rnam pa ni// snying pa'i dkyil da 'khor dang mnyam par// dgu ban+d+ha ru ni rnam dgos te// dgra'i dkyil 'khor dor bar bya// tha mar khams dang ldan pa yi// dkyil 'khor lngas ni// 
11a6(rgyud): ldan pa dang // kha dog lnga dang yang dag ldan// dgra blun par ni rtag par gyi// lta ba lnga po grang dga' che// kha dog lnga'i de bzhin gshegs// sangs rgyas lnga dang mnyam sbyor bas// sa nI
11a7(rgyud): mtshan gyis rab tu sbyar// dkyil 'khor lnga'i dbus su ni// sangs rgyas ldan dgod par bya// kha dog lnga dang ting 'dzin gyis// 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga yis khyab// shel dang ba zla ba'i 'dra rma
11a8(rgyud): sangs rgyas thas cid gcig stug/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnam snang mdzad// dpa' ba'i sa ba de bzhin gshegs// i ni 'dra na 'i 'od 'dra zhing // rdo rje rjes cad gcig sus pa/ mi skyong
11b1(rgyud): shes lngas byung ba// rdo rje'i ltas pa de bzhin gshegs// 'dzam bu'i gser gi 'od 'dra zhing // sangs rgyas thas cad gcig sdus pa// sems can kun gyi don du 'byung // 'bar ba'i/ 
11b2(rgyud): lta ba de bzhin gshegs// dpa'o chen po pad ma 'dra// pad+ma ma ra ga'i nor bu'i 'od// chos kyi ye shes las byung ba// chags pa'i lte bu de bzhin gshegs// mAr rgad kyi ni 'dog 'dra zhing / rdza dang
11b3(rgyud): sangs rgyas thas cad gcig smras pa// sangs rgyas kun 'jig las byung ba// byams pa'i lci ba de bzhin gshegs// dbus su ma sra'i bzhi dag pa// nor bu chu shel 'dog 'dra ba// shar phyogs tem/ 
11b4(rgyud): tu sngon po che// lho ru ser po yang dag ldan// nub phyir der/ ni dmar po ste// byang du ljang khu yang dgra ldan// kun du khas dang ldan pa la// sgor nu khyams dang bral ba'o// gang zhig dbus
11b5(rgyud): mAr yang dag bshad// sangs ye shes bla med ya ni// gzhan dag don kun yang dag ldan// ting 'dzin ye shes dam pa yin// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas pas// bzla ba'i
11b6(rgyud): dkyil 'khor dam pa bsamA// sangs rgyas kun ni rnam sgoms la// spyan ni dbus su bsam par bya// bzhin bzangs spyan ni yangs pa dang // nor bu chu shel mdog 'dra la// mtshan rnams thas cad yongs
11b7(rgyud): su rdzogs// bud med sgyu ma'i mchog 'dzin la// phyag tu 'khor lo sgom bya ste// khams gsum pa na dbang byed pa// dngos grub kun byed ye shes ni// 'khor lo yid bzhin nor bu mdog/ nam mkha' rdo
11b8(rgyud): rje dbus chung par// bzla ba'i dkyil 'khor dam pa bas ma// sangs rgyas sku ni rnam sgom la// nam mkha'i rdo rje mchog sgom mo// zhal mdzes spyan ni yangs pa dang // ud pal sngon pa'i medab ma'i 'dog
12a1(rgyud): mtshan rnams thas cad yang dag rdzogs// na mkha'i sgyu ma'i mchog bas mos// phyag tu ud pal sngon po ste// khams gsuM pas ni phyag byas pa// sangs rgyas byang chub byed pa 'i
12a2(rgyud): mchog/ gsang ba'i dngos grub rdo rje can// na mkha' rdo rje dbus chud par// bzla ba'i dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam// sangs rgyas sku ni rnam skom la// rdo rje chos mar rnam par bsam
12a3(rgyud): mdzes pa'i zhal ni spyan yangs pa // pad ma ra ga lta bu'i'i dge/ sku 'dog dmar po yang dag 'byung // chags pa'i pad ma mdzi na stug pa// mtshan rnams thos cad yang dag rdzog/ rgyan rnams
12a4(rgyud): kun gyis rnam par rgyan// phyag tu ud pal dmar pa ni// sangs rgyas thas cad rab sgoms pa'o// chos kyi ye shes byed dpe 'chog/ gsang ba dam tshig rdo rje can// mkha'i dbyings rdo rje/ 
12a5(rgyud): dbus chud pa// bzla ba'i dkyil 'khor dam pa sgom// sangs rgyas gzugs ni rnams sgom la// sgrol ma mchog ni bsam par bya// zhal mdzes sbyin na yangs pa dang // sna tshog
12a6(rgyud): rgyun gyis rnam par rgya ni// klu kha dog ser po nyid byas ma zhing // bud med sgyu ma'i dregs rdo ba// phyag tu ud pal dam pa ni// ser po snang ba bsam par bya// rdo rje 'dri 'dzin las byung ba// sems can kun

12b7(rgyud): 'jig rten du rgyud rab gsungs// sgra nyid gsang sngags tshul gyis ni/ dngas grub thas cad rtsol mdzad pa// sngags pas de nyid snyoms nas ni// de grub na ni 'gyur 'gyur te// sngags pa lus

13a1(rgyud): bzhin+da nor bu ltar// rtag tu sems can don byed do// de ltar mkhyen nas thugs rjes non// rdo rje 'chang bsregs kyis zhus tshe// grub pa'i snang sngags sdus pa ni// 'gro ba'i

13a8(rgyud): la sogs pa'i 'chu 'ching bar byed do// skyed mos tshal lam/ zhing la bya dang 'bru dang srin dang / byi ba rnams kyis nye bar 'che ba bzlog par byed do// du khrod kyi ras la ming dang bcas pa'i sngags bris la
13b1(rgyud): sra tshil gis btums te/ dur khrod kyi bum par bcug nas kha bcad te// de nyid du spras pas mdal rengs par 'gyuraro// phyung nas 'o mas bkrus te/ chul po bas zhi bar 'gyuraro//

13b6(rgyud): pa'i kha rengs par byed do// skye 'am dpung pa la btab na/ g.yul ngogs kyi mtshon cha dpal zhi bar 'gyuraro// grog 'khar gyi 'byim pa las/ byis pa'i// tshogs kyi bdag po'i rkang pa'i mthil
13b7(rgyud): du sngags kyi rgyal po 'di bcug skye// bzhi mdor sbas na 'gro ba dang // 'ong ba thams cad rengs par byed cing / rtag par byed pa thams cad rengs par byed do// gro ga 'am gos la sngag
13b8(rgyud): kyi rgyal po 'di bris la// sna tshol gI btums te de nyid kyi khog par bcug la/ bum pa gsar pa chus bkang ba'i nang du bcug na/ yongs su rtag pa rengs par byed do// bla gro kyi mtha' ma/ 
14a1(rgyud): la sngags rje su dran zhing 'dud pa bcings pas/ lam du rkun ma la sogs rengs par byed cing // nags kyi ban la sogs par can dang // mche ba can rnams rengs par byed/ 
14a2(rgyud): de bong ba lA lan bdun sngags te/ chur ba cug ma n+ya na rgyu ba'i kha 'ching bar byed do// dur khrod kyi ras la pha rol gyi dpung gi tshigs kyi skyes bu'i btso bo'i ming spros pa'i sngags sna tshogs rdo rje
14a3(rgyud): dbus su bris la/ sna tshogs rdo rje'i phyi rol tu yi gi lam rgyad bris shing / phyi rol dbang chen gyi dkyil 'khor dang // ldan par bral te/ phyogs rdo rjes rgyan pa'i sgra tshil las byas pa'i tshogs kyi
14a4(rgyud): bdagu pa'i khog par bcug pa'i sngags phyi rol gi dpung gitshogs kyi rdzas 'tshams kyi bar tu bcug na/ dpung gi tshigs rengs par byed do// sngags oM gnyis ka sbyar du btsug la

14a8(rgyud): byed do// man chung gi rtse mang du btsangs ste/ sngags rji pas skyigs bu me par byo gatham pal mngon par sngagasungs/ m-i 'das pa ses par byengs rlos 'i mnaso pa rnams
14b1(rgyud): ras kyi dum bral dris te/ khyim gang gi skor bdags pa'i khyim der b+h+yam bu la sogs pa rnam para'i rgyong bzlog par byed do// dang / sha dang / chang dang / nas rgya su sngags pas grong khyer

14b3(rgyud): byed do// gang 'ga' zhig la grong la sogs pa sbyin par 'gyur ba la bzlas pa tsam gris zlog par byed do// rtag tu bzlas na da lta drang lha ma yin dang / lho mche chen po rnams kyi len bdun
14b4(rgyud): 'gyur ro// dpal rje btsun sangs rgyas bco ldan 'das man par byang chub pa'i dus su bdud pa ni las/ brgyal bar bya ba'i don du/ sngags kyi rgyal po 'di mdzad sgyu myi snyan pa
14b5(rgyud): ba'i phyir/ mdzod skye'i nir bu zhes bye bar grags pa yin no// sog mo la mngon par sngags te/ gtor bas/ sbrul dag bye ro bar byed do// khyi me ga rtsig si la rdo rgyus la mngon par sngags pas
14b6(rgyud): bris na/ sbrul gyi zil gyis non par mi 'gyur ro// yang rdo le ba la sngags bzong bus bkros te/ bris lnga sbas na/ ri dgas dang / sbrul bdug pa nas khyim 'am/ grong ngam/ grong khyer du sbas na ji srid 'ad
